{

    u_xlat7.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;

    u_xlat16_8.xyz = min(u_xlat16_8.xyz, vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005));
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat10.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat10_4.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat10_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_32);
    u_xlat16_0.w = u_xlat10_3.w * _CustomAlpha;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * _EmisssionColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat10_4.zzz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat4.x = _TimeParameters.x * _DOTEmissionQuency;
    u_xlat4.y = _TimeParameters.x * _OverlayColorQuency;
    u_xlat4.xy = sin(u_xlat4.xy);
    u_xlat16_32 = _OverlayColor.w + (-_OverlayColorFlicker);
    u_xlat16_35 = _OverlayColor.w + _OverlayColorFlicker;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 + (-u_xlat16_35);
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat4.y * u_xlat16_32 + u_xlat16_35;
    u_xlat16_32 = (-u_xlat16_32) * _Ratio_OverlayColorEffect + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_32) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = _OverlayColor.xyz * vec3(_Ratio_OverlayColorEffect) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_32 = (-u_xlat16_31) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_32 = log2(u_xlat16_32);
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_32 * _DOTFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * _flowFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_32 = exp2(u_xlat16_32);
    u_xlat16_32 = min(u_xlat16_32, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_35 = exp2(u_xlat16_35);
    u_xlat16_35 = min(u_xlat16_35, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_8.x = (-_DOTEmissionMax) + _DOTEmissionMin;
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat4.x * u_xlat16_8.x + _DOTEmissionMax;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_32) * _flowFresnelColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = _flowColor.xyz * _flowColor.www + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_35 * _DOTEmissionScale;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * _Ratio_FlashColorEffect;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_32) * _DOTColor.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xy = vs_TEXCOORD8.xy * _AddTexST.xy + _AddTexST.zw;
    u_xlat24 = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat4.xy = vec2(u_xlat24) * _flowPosition.zw + u_xlat4.xy;
    u_xlat10_4.xyz = texture2D(_AdditionalTexture, u_xlat4.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat10_4.xyz * _AddTexColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_32 = _Ratio_ExtraTexture * _AddTexScale;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_32) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * vec3(vec3(_Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor)) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * _SteadyColor.xyz + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = _Ratio_SteadyColorEffect * _SteadyColor.w;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(0.300000012, 0.300000012, 0.300000012) + vec3(0.699999988, 0.699999988, 0.699999988);
    u_xlat16_31 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_31);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.w = (-u_xlat16_1.x) * 1.5 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.w = clamp(u_xlat16_3.w, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_1 = (-u_xlat16_0) + u_xlat16_3;
    u_xlat16_0 = vec4(_WhiteFresnelAlpha) * u_xlat16_1 + u_xlat16_0;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_0.w;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat6.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz / u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = min(u_xlat4.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    return;
}

    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;

in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
float u_xlat6;
float u_xlat11;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + u_xlat6;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.y = u_xlat1.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat11 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_2.xy = max(u_xlat1.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_2.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyw = (-u_xlat4.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat1.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat1.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat4.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat4.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat4.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat0.z * unity_FogParams.z + unity_FogParams.w;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat3.x = min(max(u_xlat3.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat3.x = clamp(u_xlat3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    gl_Position = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.x = u_xlat3.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.yzw = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _AdditionalTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
float u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
vec3 u_xlat6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_9;
vec3 u_xlat10;
float u_xlat14;
mediump float u_xlat16_15;
float u_xlat24;
mediump float u_xlat16_31;
mediump float u_xlat16_32;
mediump float u_xlat16_33;
mediump float u_xlat16_35;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyw = u_xlat16_1.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyw;
    u_xlat16_31 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_31);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_2.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_2.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat0 = max(u_xlat0, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0 = inversesqrt(u_xlat0);
    u_xlat10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat0) * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_31 = dot((-u_xlat10.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_31 + u_xlat16_31;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_31)) + (-u_xlat10.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat10.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = abs(u_xlat16_31) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_31 = min(u_xlat16_31, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_4.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_32 = max(u_xlat16_32, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_32 = min(u_xlat16_32, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_33 = (-u_xlat16_32) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_32 * u_xlat16_33;
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_33 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_3 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_33);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_3.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_5.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = max(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_5.x = log2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_5.x = exp2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_32 * u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat16_35 + 1.0;
    u_xlat10.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat10.x;
    u_xlat10.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat10.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_15 = (-u_xlat16_5.x) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_5.x = min(max(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_5.x = clamp(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_15 = (-u_xlat16_15) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_15 = (-u_xlat16_32) + u_xlat16_15;
    u_xlat4.x = u_xlat16_32 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_15 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_32 = min(max(u_xlat16_32, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_32 = clamp(u_xlat16_32, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xxx * u_xlat6.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-u_xlat16_3.xyz) * u_xlat16_5.xxx + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_32) + (-u_xlat6.xyz);
    u_xlat14 = (-u_xlat16_31) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat14 * u_xlat14;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_32) * u_xlat7.xyz + u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat10.xyz = u_xlat10.xyz * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat10.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat10.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat0) + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat0) + vec3(-0.200000003, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat0 = inversesqrt(u_xlat0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat0) * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat0 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0 = min(max(u_xlat0, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0 = clamp(u_xlat0, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat14 = (-u_xlat0) * u_xlat0 + 1.0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 * u_xlat0 + u_xlat14;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat16_35 / u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 * u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 * u_xlat4.x;
    u_xlat0 = min(u_xlat0, 100.0);
    u_xlat6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat0) * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat0 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0 = min(max(u_xlat0, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0 = clamp(u_xlat0, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat0) * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat0) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = min(u_xlat16_8.xyz, vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005));
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat10.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_4.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_32);
    u_xlat16_0.w = u_xlat16_3.w * _CustomAlpha;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * _EmisssionColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_4.zzz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat4.x = _TimeParameters.x * _DOTEmissionQuency;
    u_xlat4.y = _TimeParameters.x * _OverlayColorQuency;
    u_xlat4.xy = sin(u_xlat4.xy);
    u_xlat16_32 = _OverlayColor.w + (-_OverlayColorFlicker);
    u_xlat16_35 = _OverlayColor.w + _OverlayColorFlicker;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 + (-u_xlat16_35);
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat4.y * u_xlat16_32 + u_xlat16_35;
    u_xlat16_32 = (-u_xlat16_32) * _Ratio_OverlayColorEffect + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_32) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = _OverlayColor.xyz * vec3(_Ratio_OverlayColorEffect) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_32 = (-u_xlat16_31) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_32 = log2(u_xlat16_32);
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_32 * _DOTFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * _flowFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_32 = exp2(u_xlat16_32);
    u_xlat16_32 = min(u_xlat16_32, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_35 = exp2(u_xlat16_35);
    u_xlat16_35 = min(u_xlat16_35, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_8.x = (-_DOTEmissionMax) + _DOTEmissionMin;
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat4.x * u_xlat16_8.x + _DOTEmissionMax;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_32) * _flowFresnelColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = _flowColor.xyz * _flowColor.www + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_35 * _DOTEmissionScale;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * _Ratio_FlashColorEffect;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_32) * _DOTColor.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xy = vs_TEXCOORD8.xy * _AddTexST.xy + _AddTexST.zw;
    u_xlat24 = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat4.xy = vec2(u_xlat24) * _flowPosition.zw + u_xlat4.xy;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = texture(_AdditionalTexture, u_xlat4.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * _AddTexColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_32 = _Ratio_ExtraTexture * _AddTexScale;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_32) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * vec3(vec3(_Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor)) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * _SteadyColor.xyz + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = _Ratio_SteadyColorEffect * _SteadyColor.w;

    u_xlat16_34 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_34);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_34) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_2.w = (-u_xlat16_1.x) * 1.5 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.w = clamp(u_xlat16_2.w, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_1 = (-u_xlat16_0) + u_xlat16_2;
    u_xlat16_0 = vec4(_WhiteFresnelAlpha) * u_xlat16_1 + u_xlat16_0;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_0.w;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz / u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = min(u_xlat5.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz;
    return;
}

void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + u_xlat6;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.y = u_xlat1.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat11 + 0.125;

    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz;

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _AdditionalTexture;

UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
bool u_xlatb2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
vec3 u_xlat8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
vec3 u_xlat13;
float u_xlat16;
mediump float u_xlat16_17;
float u_xlat24;
mediump float u_xlat16_34;
mediump float u_xlat16_36;
mediump float u_xlat16_37;
mediump float u_xlat16_39;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyw = u_xlat16_1.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyw;
    u_xlat16_34 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_34 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_34);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_34) * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_3.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_3.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat13.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_34 = dot((-u_xlat13.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_34 = u_xlat16_34 + u_xlat16_34;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_34)) + (-u_xlat13.xyz);
    u_xlat16_34 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat13.xyz);
    u_xlat16_34 = abs(u_xlat16_34) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_34 = min(u_xlat16_34, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_5 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_5.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_36 = max(u_xlat16_36, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_36 = min(u_xlat16_36, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_36) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_36 * u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_4 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_4.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_6.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_6.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_6.x = max(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_6.x = log2(u_xlat16_6.x);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_6.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_6.x = exp2(u_xlat16_6.x);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_6.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xxx;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_36 * u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat13.x = u_xlat16_39 * u_xlat16_39 + 1.0;
    u_xlat13.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat13.x;
    u_xlat13.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat13.xxx;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_5.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_17 = (-u_xlat16_6.x) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_6.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_6.x = min(max(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_6.x = clamp(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_17 = (-u_xlat16_17) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_17 = (-u_xlat16_36) + u_xlat16_17;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat16_36 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_17 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_36 = min(max(u_xlat16_36, 0.0), 1.0);
#else

    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_32) + (-u_xlat6.xyz);
    u_xlat14 = (-u_xlat16_31) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat14 * u_xlat14;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_32) * u_xlat7.xyz + u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat10.xyz = u_xlat10.xyz * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat10.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat10.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat0) + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat0) + vec3(-0.200000003, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat0 = inversesqrt(u_xlat0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat0) * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat0 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat0 = clamp(u_xlat0, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat14 = (-u_xlat0) * u_xlat0 + 1.0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 * u_xlat0 + u_xlat14;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat16_35 / u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 * u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 * u_xlat4.x;
    u_xlat0 = min(u_xlat0, 100.0);
    u_xlat6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat0) * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat0 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat0 = clamp(u_xlat0, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat0) * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat0) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0 = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, vs_TEXCOORD7.xy).x;
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlat0<vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
    u_xlat16_32 = (u_xlatb0) ? 0.0 : _MainLightShadowParams.x;
    u_xlat16_35 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 + u_xlat16_35;
    u_xlatb0 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
    u_xlatb4 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb0 || u_xlatb4;
    u_xlat16_32 = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat7.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_32) * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = min(u_xlat16_8.xyz, vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005));
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat10.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat10_4.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat10_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_32);
    u_xlat16_0.w = u_xlat10_3.w * _CustomAlpha;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * _EmisssionColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat10_4.zzz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat4.x = _TimeParameters.x * _DOTEmissionQuency;
    u_xlat4.y = _TimeParameters.x * _OverlayColorQuency;
    u_xlat4.xy = sin(u_xlat4.xy);
    u_xlat16_32 = _OverlayColor.w + (-_OverlayColorFlicker);
    u_xlat16_35 = _OverlayColor.w + _OverlayColorFlicker;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 + (-u_xlat16_35);
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat4.y * u_xlat16_32 + u_xlat16_35;
    u_xlat16_32 = (-u_xlat16_32) * _Ratio_OverlayColorEffect + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_32) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = _OverlayColor.xyz * vec3(_Ratio_OverlayColorEffect) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_32 = (-u_xlat16_31) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_32 = log2(u_xlat16_32);
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_32 * _DOTFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * _flowFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_32 = exp2(u_xlat16_32);
    u_xlat16_32 = min(u_xlat16_32, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_35 = exp2(u_xlat16_35);
    u_xlat16_35 = min(u_xlat16_35, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_8.x = (-_DOTEmissionMax) + _DOTEmissionMin;
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat4.x * u_xlat16_8.x + _DOTEmissionMax;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_32) * _flowFresnelColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = _flowColor.xyz * _flowColor.www + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_35 * _DOTEmissionScale;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * _Ratio_FlashColorEffect;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_32) * _DOTColor.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xy = vs_TEXCOORD8.xy * _AddTexST.xy + _AddTexST.zw;
    u_xlat24 = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat4.xy = vec2(u_xlat24) * _flowPosition.zw + u_xlat4.xy;
    u_xlat10_4.xyz = texture2D(_AdditionalTexture, u_xlat4.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat10_4.xyz * _AddTexColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_32 = _Ratio_ExtraTexture * _AddTexScale;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_32) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * vec3(vec3(_Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor)) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * _SteadyColor.xyz + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = _Ratio_SteadyColorEffect * _SteadyColor.w;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(0.300000012, 0.300000012, 0.300000012) + vec3(0.699999988, 0.699999988, 0.699999988);
    u_xlat16_31 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_31);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.w = (-u_xlat16_1.x) * 1.5 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.w = clamp(u_xlat16_3.w, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_1 = (-u_xlat16_0) + u_xlat16_3;
    u_xlat16_0 = vec4(_WhiteFresnelAlpha) * u_xlat16_1 + u_xlat16_0;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_0.w;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat6.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz / u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = min(u_xlat4.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    return;
}

void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + u_xlat6;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.y = u_xlat1.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat11 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_2.xy = max(u_xlat1.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_2.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyw = (-u_xlat4.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat1.x;

    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;

    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);

{

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyw;

    u_xlat16_3.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_3.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;

    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat13.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_34 = dot((-u_xlat13.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);

    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_36 * u_xlat16_36;

    u_xlat16 = (-u_xlat16_34) + 1.0;

    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 * u_xlat16_36;

    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);

    u_xlat16_9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * u_xlat8.xyz;

    u_xlat2.y = _TimeParameters.x * _OverlayColorQuency;

    u_xlat16_36 = _OverlayColor.w + (-_OverlayColorFlicker);
    u_xlat16_39 = _OverlayColor.w + _OverlayColorFlicker;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 + (-u_xlat16_39);
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat2.y * u_xlat16_36 + u_xlat16_39;

    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 * _flowFresnelPower;

    u_xlat16_36 = min(u_xlat16_36, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_39 = exp2(u_xlat16_39);

    u_xlat16_9.x = (-_DOTEmissionMax) + _DOTEmissionMin;
    u_xlat16_9.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat16_9.x + _DOTEmissionMax;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_39 * u_xlat16_9.x;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 * u_xlat16_9.x;

    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_39 * _DOTEmissionScale;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 * _Ratio_FlashColorEffect;

float u_xlat11;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + u_xlat6;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.y = u_xlat1.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat11 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_2.xy = max(u_xlat1.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_2.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyw = (-u_xlat4.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat1.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat1.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat4.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat4.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat4.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;

UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;

in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
bool u_xlatb2;

mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;

mediump float u_xlat16_34;
mediump float u_xlat16_36;
mediump float u_xlat16_37;
mediump float u_xlat16_39;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb2){discard;}
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyw = u_xlat16_1.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyw;
    u_xlat16_34 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_34 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_34);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_34) * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_3.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_3.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat13.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_34 = dot((-u_xlat13.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_34 = u_xlat16_34 + u_xlat16_34;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_34)) + (-u_xlat13.xyz);
    u_xlat16_34 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat13.xyz);
    u_xlat16_34 = abs(u_xlat16_34) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_34 = min(u_xlat16_34, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_5 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_5.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_36 = max(u_xlat16_36, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_36 = min(u_xlat16_36, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_36) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_36 * u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_4 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_37);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_4.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_6.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_6.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_6.x = max(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_6.x = log2(u_xlat16_6.x);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_6.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_6.x = exp2(u_xlat16_6.x);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_6.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xxx;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_36 * u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat13.x = u_xlat16_39 * u_xlat16_39 + 1.0;
    u_xlat13.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat13.x;
    u_xlat13.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat13.xxx;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_5.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_17 = (-u_xlat16_6.x) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_6.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_6.x = min(max(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_6.x = clamp(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_17 = (-u_xlat16_17) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_17 = (-u_xlat16_36) + u_xlat16_17;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat16_36 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_17 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_36 = min(max(u_xlat16_36, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_36 = clamp(u_xlat16_36, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) * u_xlat16_6.xxx + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) + (-u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat16 = (-u_xlat16_34) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16 * u_xlat16;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 * u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * u_xlat8.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat13.xyz = u_xlat13.xyz * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat13.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat13.xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + vec3(-0.200000003, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat8.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2.x = min(max(u_xlat2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16 = (-u_xlat2.x) * u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_39 * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x + u_xlat16;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_39 / u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat2.x = min(u_xlat2.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat2.x = min(max(u_xlat2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(vs_TEXCOORD7.xy,vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
    u_xlat16_2.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_36 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_2.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_36;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb5 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb5 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb2 = u_xlatb2 || u_xlatb5;
    u_xlat16_36 = (u_xlatb2) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat8.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = min(u_xlat16_9.xyz, vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005));
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xyz + u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat13.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_5.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_36);
    u_xlat16_0.w = u_xlat16_0.w * _CustomAlpha;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * _EmisssionColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat16_5.zzz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = _TimeParameters.x * _DOTEmissionQuency;
    u_xlat2.y = _TimeParameters.x * _OverlayColorQuency;
    u_xlat2.xy = sin(u_xlat2.xy);
    u_xlat16_36 = _OverlayColor.w + (-_OverlayColorFlicker);
    u_xlat16_39 = _OverlayColor.w + _OverlayColorFlicker;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 + (-u_xlat16_39);
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat2.y * u_xlat16_36 + u_xlat16_39;
    u_xlat16_36 = (-u_xlat16_36) * _Ratio_OverlayColorEffect + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = _OverlayColor.xyz * vec3(_Ratio_OverlayColorEffect) + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_36 = (-u_xlat16_34) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_36 = log2(u_xlat16_36);
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_36 * _DOTFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 * _flowFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_36 = exp2(u_xlat16_36);
    u_xlat16_36 = min(u_xlat16_36, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_39 = exp2(u_xlat16_39);
    u_xlat16_39 = min(u_xlat16_39, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_9.x = (-_DOTEmissionMax) + _DOTEmissionMin;
    u_xlat16_9.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat16_9.x + _DOTEmissionMax;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_39 * u_xlat16_9.x;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 * u_xlat16_9.x;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * _flowFresnelColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = _flowColor.xyz * _flowColor.www + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_39 * _DOTEmissionScale;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 * _Ratio_FlashColorEffect;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * _DOTColor.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xy = vs_TEXCOORD8.xy * _AddTexST.xy + _AddTexST.zw;
    u_xlat24 = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat2.xy = vec2(u_xlat24) * _flowPosition.zw + u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_AdditionalTexture, u_xlat2.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * _AddTexColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_36 = _Ratio_ExtraTexture * _AddTexScale;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_36) + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * vec3(vec3(_Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor)) + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_34) * _SteadyColor.xyz + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_34 = _Ratio_SteadyColorEffect * _SteadyColor.w;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_34) * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(0.300000012, 0.300000012, 0.300000012) + vec3(0.699999988, 0.699999988, 0.699999988);
    u_xlat16_34 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_34 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_34);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_34) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_2.w = (-u_xlat16_1.x) * 1.5 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_2.w = min(max(u_xlat16_2.w, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_2.w = clamp(u_xlat16_2.w, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_1 = (-u_xlat16_0) + u_xlat16_2;
    u_xlat16_0 = vec4(_WhiteFresnelAlpha) * u_xlat16_1 + u_xlat16_0;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_0.w;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz / u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = min(u_xlat5.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz;
    return;
}

#endif
"

"// hash: 2ae351e8acbca6e3
#ifdef VERTEX
#version 100

uniform 	vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;

uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
attribute highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
attribute highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
varying highp float vs_TEXCOORD0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
float u_xlat6;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD0 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    return;
}

    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;

    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);

    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 * _ShadowBias.y;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat6) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;

in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
float u_xlat6;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _LightDirection.xyz * _ShadowBias.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat6 = dot(_LightDirection.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat6 = min(max(u_xlat6, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat6 = (-u_xlat6) + 1.0;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 * _ShadowBias.y;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat6) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;

    gl_Position.z = max((-u_xlat0.w), u_xlat0.z);
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat0.xyw;
    return;
}
